5c:["$","$L2e",null,{"type":"tip","title":"Intuition: Why the Markov property matters","children":["$","p",null,{"style":{"fontSize":"1rem","color":"var(--text-body)","lineHeight":1.75,"marginBottom":"1.25em","marginTop":0},"children":["The Markov property is a ",["$","strong",null,{"style":{"color":"var(--text-strong)","fontWeight":600},"children":"compression claim"}],": it says that no matter how long the history, the current state contains all predictive power about the future. This is what makes sequential decision making tractable. Without it, the value of a state would depend on an unbounded past, and no finite representation of \"value\" would exist. The price of this compression is that you must engineer your state to be sufficient for prediction."]}]}]

5f:["$","p",null,{"style":{"fontSize":"1rem","color":"var(--text-body)","lineHeight":1.75,"marginBottom":"1.25em","marginTop":0},"children":"Consider a robot that observes only joint positions but not joint velocities. The next\nstate depends on the current velocity, which is not in the observation. Two robots at the\nsame position but different velocities will transition to different next states, so the\ntransition is non-Markov in the observed state. A language model that receives only the\nmost recent token cannot distinguish \"The bank charges fees\" from \"The bank slopes gently\"\n— the same token (\"bank\") with entirely different meaning depending on history. c1:["$","p",null,{"style":{"fontSize":"1rem","color":"var(--text-body)","lineHeight":1.75,"marginBottom":"1.25em","marginTop":0},"children":["The key technical challenge in offline ",["$","$L2f",null,{"term":"RL"}]," is ",["$","strong",null,{"style":{"color":"var(--text-strong)","fontWeight":600},"children":"distributional shift"}],": the learned policy\nmay assign high value to state-action pairs that are rare or absent in the dataset.\nWithout the ability to collect new experience, these value estimates cannot be corrected,\nleading to overoptimistic Q-values and unstable policy improvement. e5:["$","p",null,{"style":{"fontSize":"1rem","color":"var(--text-body)","lineHeight":1.75,"marginBottom":"1.25em","marginTop":0},"children":[["$","strong",null,{"style":{"color":"var(--text-strong)","fontWeight":600},"children":["5.
